(Tokyo) It is reported that the Japanese government has proposed to the Soviet Russian government to jointly withdraw military equipment from the border between the two countries. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs issued the following opinion: When Ambassador Ota stationed in Russia met with Stromnikov on August 30, he pointed out that Russian aircraft often crossed the border and that strange incidents often occurred. The borders between the United States and Canada have established peaceful relations because they are undefended. On the contrary, disputes have occurred on the border between France and Germany due to military equipment. In order to maintain peace on the border, it was said that Russia has recently needed to withdraw the military facilities added to the border area, arousing Russia's attention. However, there was no concrete proposal such as applying the Treaty of Portsmouth. As for the conclusion of a non-aggression treaty proposed by the Russian side, because both countries have signed the Kellogg-Briand Pact, the timing is not yet ripe, and reservations have been made. However, the Japanese government has proposed the establishment of a joint border commission, which will peacefully resolve disputes occurring on the border. The Russian side has no objection in principle to this proposal, so Russia should also consider withdrawing the Red Army from the border with Manchuria on its own initiative. (20th Electric Communication Telegram)

Japan Wants to Establish Automobile Industry 47

Because It Has a Major Relationship with Military Affairs

(Tokyo) The Ministry of the Army, in view of the important relationship between the domestic automobile industry and national defense, proposed a plan to establish the automobile industry. Representatives from the Ministries of Commerce and Industry, Finance, Interior, Railways, and the Army held a joint meeting on the 19th, but failed to reach a conclusion. The meeting will be reopened on the 28th to formally determine the government's automobile administrative policy. (20th Japanese Allied Telegram)

If the Eastern European Convention Fails, Russia and France May Conclude an Alliance 48

Before Bartou Left Geneva to Return Home

He Had a Meeting with Litvinov

(Geneva) Although Soviet Russia has joined the stage of Geneva, it wants to play its own tune. It is heard that this is the main point of the speech made by Russian representative Litvinov at a private banquet today, with French Foreign Minister Bartou also present. It is rumored that the Foreign Ministers of Russia and France are currently negotiating a mutual assistance treaty between Russia and France to replace the current failed Eastern Locarno Treaty. However, inquiries were made everywhere at 4:00 p.m. today, and this statement has not been confirmed. Although France advocates that any treaty must not go beyond the scope of the League of Nations treaty, such a treaty is not absolutely impossible. Bartou resumed negotiations with Litvinov this evening and has set off to return to Paris. (19th Reuters Telegram)

(Paris) The rumors circulating outside that France is currently negotiating a bilateral agreement with Russia were all laughed off by well-informed circles today. According to the responsible parties, French diplomats have no intention of abandoning the Eastern European Mutual Assistance Convention, and will proceed even if Germany and Poland are unwilling to join. In addition to France and Russia, the supporters of this treaty also include the Little Entente countries, Turkey, Greece, or other Baltic countries. However, France and Russia must first reach an understanding to form the basis for this huge structure. (20th Reuters Telegram)

(Paris) Foreign Minister Bartou returned to the country from Geneva and arrived here this morning, declaring to reporters from the Paris Afternoon News that the main purpose of his trip to Geneva was to get the Soviet Union to join the League of Nations. This attempt was necessary but quite difficult. He will go to Geneva again at the end of the next period to develop the results he has obtained. (20th Havas Telegram)

Press Association in Geneva Hosts Banquet for Councilors of the League of Nations 49

Bartou Delivers a Speech

Saying that the Soviet Union's Joining the League Is Beneficial to World Peace

To Achieve Disarmament, One Must First Reshape People's Hearts

(Geneva) The League of Nations News Association, organized by newspaper reporters from various countries stationed in Geneva, hosts a banquet for the executive councilors of the League of Nations and the president of the League of Nations General Assembly once a year. The League of Nations General Assembly Chairman, Swedish Foreign Minister Sandler, urged the League of Nations newspaper reporters to help the cause of peace. French Foreign Minister Bartou claimed to be a predecessor of the newspaper reporters present, saying (Regarding the duties of a reporter, there is something to be told to you. Recently, a major international event has occurred. You should comment on it from an international perspective, and you must not be confined to the views of one country. However, among you, there are those who do not follow this path and use the relations of one country as the standard for criticism, and there are also those who involve the domestic politics of one's own country with the domestic politics of other countries. This matter is known to me by the Swiss representative Morda. Morda explained to me in sincere words at the League of Nations General Assembly the reasons why Switzerland could not approve the Soviet Union's joining the League, saying that Swiss newspapers had the most severe criticism of the Soviet Union. You should know that slandering foreign countries and their representatives with words is not only a loss of the hospitality of the host, but also violates the simplest etiquette that newspaper reporters should abide by. France does not want to advise any country, nor does it want to accept the advice of any other country, especially when it comes to international integrity. I do not hesitate to say this clearly here). Speaking of the Soviet Union's joining the League, Bartou jokingly said that some people said he was the (godfather) of Russia, but he was willing to be a commoner for the Soviet Union to be stationed at the League of Nations. Bartou continued, (I and the entire French government agree to support the eight alliances of the Soviet Union. This matter is extremely difficult. Fortunately, it has been completed today. I met Litvinov at the Genoa Conference in 1922. Today's Litvinov seems to have changed his old appearance. This is what I sincerely dare to tell you. If the Soviet Union's joining the League has the danger of causing chaos and war, then we will never approve the act of joining the League. Our actions in recent days are precisely because we believe that the Soviet Union is enough to benefit peace. The world is currently going through a great panic. If the Disarmament Conference wants to work effectively, it must first reshape people's hearts and eliminate mankind's warlike psychology before it can be done) and so on. Soviet Russian Foreign Commissar Litvinov thanked the hosts and Bartou of the public banquet, and said that the international press should strive for peace. (19th Havas Telegram)

Litvinov's Remarks Arouse Repercussions in Germany 50

Saying that the Union of Russia and France Wants to Isolate Germany

The League of Nations Adopts This Strategy Only to Accelerate Its Own Collapse

(Berlin) A semi-official diplomatic commentary refuted the remarks made by Russian Foreign Minister Litvinov at the League of Nations General Assembly yesterday about the crisis of war, saying that alarming words were originally the means of Communist propaganda. Litvinov is now only trying to internationalize the anti-fascist movement. The words of Russian Foreign Minister, with their hidden meanings, are very foolish, and what he said is nothing more than the mantra of the Soviet Russian newspaper. The Russian Foreign Minister hates Germany and only wants to unite with France. When the League of Nations passed the Soviet Union's membership, the French newspaper directly said that isolating Germany was the main goal of Geneva's strategy. Litvinov's blood-spitting remarks were the first disappointment after Russia joined the League of Nations. What Germany expected was to live in peace with others. Foreign Minister Neurath said yesterday that the words of those who say that Germany is conspiring to start trouble are nothing more than malicious slanders. If the League of Nations also uses this as a strategy, it will only accelerate its collapse. (20th National Telegram)

(Berlin) The German newspapers only carried a small part of the speech given by Soviet Russian Foreign Commissar Litvinov at the League of Nations General Assembly yesterday, but we can see from the commentary in the Political and Foreign Traffic News that the German authorities have not been unaffected by some of Litvinov's words. The newspaper said, (Litvinov accused several countries without explicitly saying which countries they were. This kind of calm language is very heavy. The Soviet Union's expression of opposition to Germany is absolutely approved by France. The main meaning of the fit between Paris and Moscow should not be anything other than this. However, in our opinion, the Russian Foreign Commissar's speech has absolutely no need to use this attacking tone.) The newspaper commented on Foreign Minister Neurath's speech at the International Road Conference today, saying that (Germany has done its best to seek peace in Europe, and has made suggestions to help peace. If outsiders still accuse Germany of having war plans, then we can only say that those who say this are deliberately malicious. The League of Nations claims to maintain peace, and the method it uses is like this, and the result is only to accelerate its demise). (19th Havas Telegram)

A GlimPSE OF VARIOUS COUNTRIES' OPINIONS ON THE SOVIET UNION JOINING THE LEAGUE OF NATIONS 51

(Moscow) Newspapers worldwide are commenting on the invitation to the Soviet Union to join the League of Nations. The (Paris) *Times* stated that the major powers have already felt the necessity of cooperating and uniting with all countries in order to maintain and create peace. Some French newspapers pointed out that Litvinov's willingness to regulate the spirit of the League Covenant and the Kellogg-Briand Pact is entirely consistent with France's security proposals. The *Manchester Guardian* said that the Soviet Union's entry into the League is the most important move in history and will surely consolidate the position of peace. Romanian newspapers welcomed this new international event. The *Curentul* pointed to this as a turning point in world politics and emphasized the unity of the major powers in this event. Scandinavian newspapers regarded the invitation to the Soviet Union to join the League and to serve as a permanent council member as a major victory for Soviet diplomacy. German newspapers generally did not comment on this, but the military organ *Deutsche Wehr* expressed its frank and open anti-Soviet stance. Japanese newspapers only disclosed the invitation message without comment. The Harbin *Manchuria Daily News* took advantage of this news from Geneva to launch a new anti-Soviet attack. (TASS, 19th)

GERMAN FOREIGN MINISTER CLARIFIES DIPLOMATIC POLICY 52

Military Equality Not Achieved

Participation in Eastern European Pact Decidedly Difficult

Seeking Fair Resolution of the Saar Issue

(Berlin) At the closing of the International Road Congress, Foreign Minister Neurath delivered a lengthy speech. Yesterday's telegram mentioned that Neurath's speech touched upon the Eastern European Mutual Assistance Pact. The following is a supplementary record. Neurath said, "It is quite difficult for us to join the Eastern European Mutual Assistance Pact. According to the initiators of the pact, it seems that the purpose of the pact is only to equally guarantee the peace of all countries. However, it is generally speculated that if this pact fails, France and the Soviet Union will decide to conclude a bilateral alliance treaty. If this statement is credible, then our disapproval is even more justified." In short, Germany must first obtain the right to military equality before it can participate in the principles of the Eastern European Mutual Assistance Pact. Neurath then said that since the Treaty of Versailles in 1919, there has been a mania for concluding international treaties. Whenever something happens, treaties are used to deal with it, but this is not a good method. Regarding the Saar issue, Neurath believed that the unfairness of the peace treaty to Germany will inevitably be remedied after the plebiscite. There is no doubt about this. After the Foreign Minister, National Road Inspector Todt delivered a brief speech, stating, "You have already heard the opinions of the German political authorities. You should know that the Foreign Minister's speech today is a statement of intent to openly discuss with you various issues related to the German people." Most of the ambassadors and ministers from various countries were present. The next International Road Congress is scheduled to be held in the Netherlands in 1938. (Havas, 18th)

(Berlin) Foreign Minister Neurath spoke today at the International Road Congress here, regarding all the diplomatic and economic problems encountered by the German government, saying that Germany's diplomatic policy is entirely dedicated to peace. What Germans need is friendship with other countries, thereby consolidating the work of the National Socialist government and making it last far into the future. We now put forward two positive demands that we insist on and must realize: (1) Regarding armaments, we must receive equal treatment. (2) The resolution of the Saar issue must be in accordance with the provisions of the Treaty of Versailles and its political reasons. The reason why Germany withdrew from the League of Nations was because it failed to obtain equal status. Establishing equal rights is the indispensable foundation for cooperation between Germany and other countries. If the League of Nations is to become a true organization for maintaining peace in the future, then far-reaching reforms are essential. The Soviet Union's entry into the League of Nations is worthy of attention in the development of the political situation. However, since we have already left the League of Nations, we do not want to discuss this matter. Although we are always pleased to see that our international affairs can obtain the cooperation of various countries. At this point, Neurath spoke about the Saar issue, saying that the core of the Saar issue has been lost to international discussion. Although France failed to force the Allied countries to allow it to annex the Saar, in 1919 France was able to separate the Saar from Germany and also obtain the coal mines of the Saar. The reason France put forward in Versailles was that the Saar residents were of mixed race and that the coal mines in southern France had been completely destroyed in the war, so it requested that the coal of the Saar be used as compensation. Today, if we discuss the value of this reason again, it will be a waste of words and will not help the matter. The Saar residents have been purely German since ancient times. This has been the case for 1,200 years. As for the coal mines, we do not want to say much. As of 1925, the coal produced in southern France was already more than before the war, and the coal paid by Germany in reparations is not included in this example. The coal Germany transported to France was also more than the total output lost by the French coal mines. France has mined a total of 180 million tons of Saar coal from 1920 to the present, while the losses suffered in the war were only 70 million tons. Even as stated in the Treaty of Versailles, it must be returned to its original owner after fifteen years. The Saar will hold a plebiscite in a few months, and at that time it will be known that the resolution of 1919 was not a fair method. What we must admit is that the return of the Saar to Germany is the only solution. Other methods are nothing more than repeating the mistake of 1919. After recently reviewing some suggestions, I have to solemnly declare that all Germans should not discuss any methods that discriminate against Germany's sovereignty, because this method will not only violate the spirit of the Treaty of Versailles, but also harm the future development of international relations. Neurath finally assured the audience that the German government is determined to protect the interests of the German people and to be a sound element in maintaining peace in Europe. (National Telegram, 19th)

LEAGUE OF NATIONS COMMITTEE MEETING 53

Outstanding Achievements in Health Cooperation with China

Debate Begins on Minority Issues

(Geneva) The Second Committee of the League of Nations (i.e., the Committee on Technical Organization Affairs) met today. The Canadian representative reported on the work of the League of Nations Health Organization in the Far East, stating that according to the latest reports received from China, the health affairs of the League of Nations in cooperation with the Chinese Economic Committee, with the Central Health Facilities Experiment Office established in Nanjing as its general office, the breadth of its business scope and the complexity of its types are quite surprising. The reporter listed in detail the work details of the Central Health Facilities Experiment Office, saying that the results were extremely excellent. (Havas, 20th)

(Geneva) At today's meeting of the Sixth Committee of the League of Nations, the Polish representative, Raczyński, proposed convening an international minority conference to draft a convention, placing all minorities on the same footing, and said that it is unfair not to give some minorities the right to express their opinions, which other minorities enjoy. Representatives from several countries agreed with this proposal. However, Swiss Foreign Minister Dr. Motta rose to say that if any country arbitrarily abandons treaties that are inconvenient to it, such as Poland's recent actions regarding minority treaties, then the League of Nations will not be able to survive for long. It is not advisable to convene a meeting as proposed by the Polish representative at this time. This kind of meeting has no hope of success from the beginning. (Reuters, 20th)

Germany Engaged in Large-Scale Aircraft Construction

French Finance Minister States Increase in Military Spending Necessary

Marseilles Lord Rothermere, leader of the British Labour Party, boarded a ship here today to go to South Africa. Germany is now building aircraft on a large scale, including the Heinkel He 70, which is powerful and being built in large numbers. He believes that if France can make all countries in the world aware that the French Air Force is ready and capable of meeting all its responsibilities, this is France's most valuable contribution to maintaining peace. (Havas, 19th)

(Geneva) French Finance Minister Germain Martin spoke here today, saying that France's international position has improved. The Soviet Union's entry into the League of Nations can help eliminate disasters. He feels that progress towards peace has never been as great as it is today. Martin said that if the international situation becomes more serious and there is a need to increase armaments, then it would be better to set up a special armament item, as in 1913, otherwise the income will eventually be insufficient to pay for military expenses. HIROTA SENDS KAWASHIMA TO MANCHURIA 58

To Investigate the Economic Reality

(Tokyo) Former Minister to Greece, Shintaro Kawashima, under the order of Foreign Minister Hirota, will go to Manchuria in early October to inspect the economic and industrial situation. Foreign Minister Hirota originally planned to establish a Joint Japan-Manchuria Economic Committee as an organization to control the economies of Japan and Manchuria. Therefore, Kawashima's mission to Manchuria seems to be to study its specific matters. (Nippon Dempo, 20th)

(Changchun) In order to unify the electricity business, the Manchurian government plans to establish the Manchurian Electric Power Joint Company. After deciding on the outlines last June, as a result of the preparations, the promoters' meeting decided on the following items on the 19th: (1) The new company is a (Manchukuo) legal entity jointly operated by Japan and Manchuria. (2) Capital is 90 million yuan. (3) Temporarily handle the electricity business in eight cities: Changchun, Fengtian, Dalian, Yingkou, Andong, Jilin, Harbin, and Qiqihar. (4) The new company does not publicly raise capital, but the (Manchukuo government) and Manchurian Electric Power Company will provide all the existing objects. (5) The Japanese and Manchurian governments will formulate laws and regulations on the electricity business within the next few days, and at the same time publish the contents. (Nippon Shokuho, 20th)

(Tokyo) This morning, the Ministry of the Imperial Household opened a disciplinary committee in the Imperial Palace to review the issue of disciplinary action against Count Fumiyoshi Tokata, who gave a speech at the Moscow Writers' Conference. As a result, the committee applied the provisions of Article 24 of the Peerage Order, recognizing that Tokata insulted the dignity of the peerage, and decided to deprive him of the rank of Count and Fourth Rank. INVESTIGATION INTO WHETHER SOVIET UNION'S RAISING OF DEBT IN THE US IS ILLEGAL 64

(Washington) The Associated Press learned today that the Justice Department is investigating whether the sale of the Soviet Union's 7% bonds in the United States violates the Johnson Act. According to the law, countries that are delinquent in paying debts to the United States may not raise debts in the United States again. Now that debt negotiations between the United States and the Soviet Union have failed, the government is paying attention to the sale of these bonds in the United States. (National Telegram, 19th)

SPANISH LEFTISTS PLOT INSURRECTION 65

Illegally Manufactured Arms Organization Broken Up

Government Confident in Its Ability to Curb the Budding Rebellion

Madrid The Spanish authorities now believe that the far-left party's insurrection is imminent, so they have implemented swift and meticulous plans to deal with any eventuality. Today, several cases of privately concealed arms and ammunition were discovered. Among the arms were flamethrowers, and clues were obtained from this. According to Prime Minister Samper, the police discovered an experimental site for illegally manufacturing explosives in the suburbs of Madrid, and a university student named Wódulski was arrested. He was found to be carrying a detailed draft of a workers' revolution plan, intending to first burn down various government offices, and then massacre people in uniforms. The Prime Minister also said that he believes that the government has the power to curb any rebellion with a large army. Tonight, a convertible car full of arms and ammunition was discovered in the University City. The public believes that the Anti-Catholic Association is now plotting to join hands with the rebel parties. The police are now intercepting cars and inspecting them in the city of Madrid. The guards of various government offices have doubled in number. The public sees the cabinet as being very stable. (Reuters, 19th)

Vienna The activities of the Austrian Communist Party are becoming increasingly serious. The authorities are now making preparations to quell the chaos. The Vienna police today searched several places suspected of being red party members and arrested eighty people. (Reuters, 19th)

CUBAN REVOLUTIONARY CONSPIRACY EXPANDS, CURRENT GOVERNMENT SHOWS SIGNS OF INSTABILITY 67

(New York) Cuba's revolutionary conspiracy is spreading widely. According to private telegrams obtained here from Santiago and Havana, opposition to the Mendieta government is increasing on all sides. The Cuban people, because revolutionary coups have long been commonplace, are also prepared to accept whatever comes. The recent hospitality shown to General Mario García Menocal, the former Cuban dictator, by President Trujillo of the Dominican Republic in Cuba's neighboring Dominican Republic, has made Cuba quite uneasy. According to news from Havana, Trujillo is suspected of funding Menocal's revolutionary conspiracy. In addition, various opposition leaders in Cuba are also eager to try. The United States government recently ordered a ban on the transportation of arms to anyone in Cuba, except for the Cuban government. This is a sign of stability. It is said that President Mendieta's position is no longer what it used to be. In the past, all parties supported Mendieta, but now they are opposing him one by one. Mendieta has repeatedly said that he will formally elect a president next January, but whether it can be implemented is still questionable. (National Telegram, 19th)

DISCORD BETWEEN ITALIAN AND SERBIAN NEWSPAPERS 68

Yugoslav Newspaper Ridicules Italian Army

Causes Protests from Rome

Rome Recently, the *Yugoslav Times* ridiculed the Battle of Caporetto during the European War (October 20, 1917, Italian troops were defeated by the German army). All the newspapers in Yugoslavia also joined in. Italian newspapers were unwilling to remain silent, so the two sides attacked each other. A few days ago, the Inter-Parliamentary Union of Commerce held a meeting in the Yugoslav capital, and Italy did not send a representative to participate, precisely because of this reason. The Italian government has recently formally protested the article in the *Yugoslav Times*. It is expected that the war of words between the two sides will end here. People here say that the two newspapers have stopped arguing for a month. Now it is a pity that Rome suddenly filed a protest out of helplessness. (Havas, 19th)

British Cotton In the Liverpool cotton market, prices fell. At 1:00 pm, the October futures price was 6.7, down 8 pounds音.

US Wheat The Chicago wheat market was affected by the rise in Liverpool. The opening price rose by .50 to .75. There was an overbought situation in the market, and sentiment remained stable. The price at 10:40 was up .25 from the opening price.

(Securities) New York Before the opening of the New York securities market, the factors favorable to the market situation were: (1) The market price of government bonds rebounded. (2) When securities prices rose, sellers seemed to be very few. People in the industry are gradually abandoning the recent short-selling concept. The general sentiment of short-sellers is now gradually decreasing. The factors unfavorable to the market situation are (1) The market situation of goods is still uncertain. (2) The trading volume has not yet expanded. Many merchants are still adopting a wait-and-see attitude. From this, it can be seen that when the securities market opened this morning, the market situation was stable, and prices fluctuated very little. However, people in the industry are still very cautious in their actions because there is no solid construction news. However, the public expects that yesterday's rise can be slightly expanded.

British Newspaper's Criticism of Huang Musong's Entry into Tibet 88

Lhasa Welcomes Mr. Huang, a Great Taboo for the British

Saying the Situation in Tibet is Extremely Urgent

Britain has always regarded Tibet as its exclusive domain. After the passing of the Dalai Lama last year, the Tibetans sent a Lama delegation to Beijing to welcome the Panchen Lama back to Tibet to preside over the government, and expressed their sincerity of inward orientation. Therefore, the Central Government specially appointed Huang Musong as an envoy to go to Tibet to express condolences and pay respects to the Dalai Lama. According to a recent telegram from Envoy Huang, he was warmly welcomed upon arriving in Lhasa, which became a great taboo for the British. Last week, the local "North China Daily News" published a London dispatch summarizing the "Times" commentary on Tibetan affairs. Its remarks were full of provocative intent. Yesterday, the newspaper reprinted a London dispatch from September 19 on this issue. The British resentment of Tibet's allegiance to the Central Government is increasingly evident, yet they still try to conceal it, which can be described as a futile attempt to cover up the truth. I have translated its telegram below for your consideration:

A reporter (from the "North China Daily News") learned that the Chinese officials in Britain were quite surprised and disappointed by the British reaction to the Chinese envoy's visit to Lhasa. They felt that General Huang Musong's mission was greatly misunderstood by the British, and their criticism was rather unfair. However, British observers of Sino-Tibetan affairs believe that General Huang's proclamation in Lhasa on September 13 was largely due to the Chinese government's desire to use the opportunity of the Dalai Lama's funeral to make a public gesture to impress the bordering territories, hoping to offset the loss of prestige caused by the loss of Manchuria. China's feelings on this matter were probably provoked by Tibet's recent increasing inclination towards India. India's trade with Tibet is now of paramount importance, while China's trade with Tibet, apart from tea, is negligible. British political observers say that in recent years, a section of the Chinese newspapers has often accused Britain of harboring ambitions to annex Tibet. Britain naturally regards this as a joke and has repeatedly solemnly denied it. However, the recent invitation from the Tibetans to Sir Charles Bell (leader of the British diplomatic mission to Lhasa in 1920) to visit Lhasa, the rising prestige of Tibetan engineer Lingong, who is believed to have studied in Rugby, England, and is building Tibet's first factory, is now purchasing British machinery to establish an electric power plant in Lhasa, and the former commander-in-chief of the Tibetan army, Longxia, who was accused of conspiring to exclude Chinese influence and was thus deprived of his eyes, all these may have aroused Nanjing's jealousy. Judging from various signs here, the situation in Tibet today is extremely tense. The reincarnation of the deceased Dalai Lama cannot be determined within two or three years. During the Dalai Lama's lifetime, he personally controlled all secular affairs. In the future, there will be no outstanding figure who can serve as the leader of Tibet for a while, and the progressive and conservative factions of the Tibetan Parliament are constantly in conflict, and it is easy for suspicions of foreign interference to arise in the Parliament.

Japanese Side Dispatches Personnel to Investigate the Miyakoshi Murder Case 89

Negotiations on this case have not yet begun

Shibayama Goes to Tianjin to Meet with Yu

Tianjin Correspondence: Miyakoshi Gozo, a Japanese merchant in the Malanyu Allied Forces, shipped a boat of goods from Tangshan on September 6, intending to supply the Japanese army in Malanyu. When he arrived at Lintoutun, at the intersection of Yutian, Fengrun, and Zunhua counties, he was mistaken for bandits by the local militia on guard. Militiaman Wu Runbi fired without authorization, killing Miyakoshi. After this incident occurred, Asami, the commander of the Japanese garrison in Tangshan, immediately protested to Tao Shangming, the Administrative Commissioner of Luan and Yu. Tao went to Ping on the 12th to discuss the matter with Shibayama. On the 13th, he came to Tianjin and visited Omaki Ryogi, the senior staff officer of the garrison army. Omaki said that it would be necessary to wait for the report from the Tangshan garrison to arrive and learn the truth before negotiations could begin. Tao returned to Tangshan on the evening of the 16th, specializing in investigating the conflict between the farmers of Fushan Temple in Qian'an and the Japanese and Korean vagrants. Negotiations on the Miyakoshi murder case were temporarily suspended. On the 13th of this month, the Tangshan branch of the Japanese Consulate General's Police Station dispatched a former senior inspector to Lintoutun, Yutian, to investigate the truth of the case. He returned to Tangshan on the 16th. According to his report, Wu Runbi, the militiaman who fired the shot, has indeed fled in fear of punishment and his whereabouts are unknown. The inspector intends to collect all relevant materials before reporting to Tianjin. Asami, the commander of the Japanese garrison in Tangshan, also dispatched 30 infantrymen led by a platoon leader to Lintoutun, Yutian, on the 16th to investigate, and returned to Tangshan on the 17th. Shibayama Kenjiro, the military attaché of the Japanese embassy, was scheduled to come to Tianjin from Ping on the 18th to visit Yu Xuezhong, the chairman of Hebei, to negotiate this matter. Before our side began negotiations, we had already recovered Miyakoshi Gozo's body and the lost one boat of goods. Chen Bao, the magistrate of Yutian County, dispatched personnel to send them to Tangshan, and then Tao Shangming forwarded them to the Japanese side. Regarding the negotiations on this case, Japanese Consul Tanaka stated to our side that he would not be responsible for the negotiations, saying that it was within the scope of the North China Garrison Army and should be negotiated directly with that department. Asami, the commander of the Japanese garrison in Tangshan, expressed a tough stance on this and demanded numerous conditions. Because Tao Shangming found the negotiations difficult, he went directly to negotiate with the North China Garrison Army, but the Japanese military department seemed to be indifferent and unwilling to negotiate with us. Shibayama, the military attaché of the Japanese embassy, went directly to Yu Xuezhong, the chairman, to negotiate, causing confusion. However, because the Japanese side had already indicated that it would discuss this issue after the Qian'an incident was resolved, our current attitude is very calm. (17th)

Jiangxi Provincial Government Implements Joint Office 90

One-third of Staff to Be Laid Off in Various Departments

Nanchang Correspondence: Chiang ordered the provincial governments in various bandit suppression areas to implement joint office to achieve unified authority. Now, Jiangxi Province has decided to implement it on the 21st. One-third of the staff is expected to be laid off from the four departments of Civil Affairs, Finance, Construction, and Education, as well as the Provincial Government Secretariat and the two Security Departments. All the saved funds will be used to strengthen county governments and lower-level organs to avoid being top-heavy and foot-light. The original order and outline of the joint office method have already been promulgated. The text of the order is as follows: (It has been verified that this government previously received the Nanchang Camp of the Military Affairs Committee's outline of the provincial government's joint office method and instructed to comply with it. We have actively prepared for it and it is now ready. Joint office will be implemented on the 21st of this month. From that day onwards, official documents to the outside world will all use the name of this government. All documents submitted by agencies directly under this government should be submitted directly to this government. However, the various departments have the authority to issue their own departmental orders regarding the supervision and direction of the operation of subordinate agencies, within the scope that does not conflict with provincial orders. In addition, the Provincial Health Department, Land Bureau, and Provincial Disaster Relief Association should be guided by the Civil Affairs Department, the Bandit Suppression Post-Disaster Donation Management Bureau should be guided by the Finance Department, and the Rural Cooperation Committee and the Agricultural College should be guided by the Construction Department. The Nanchang and Jiujiang Municipal Committees and the Lushan Administration should be guided by their respective competent authorities. In addition to submitting separate reports and orders, a copy of the camp's instructions and the outline of the provincial government's joint office method is issued for your compliance. This order.) (September 14th)

Analysis of the Naval Conference by Japan (Japanese Correspondence) 91

Great Powers in the Eyes of the Japanese

Preparations in Foreign Policy

The so-called crisis of 1936 was first proclaimed by Japan, and it tried its best to artificially deepen its extent. Now 1936 is almost upon us. After the first failure of the London Naval Preparatory Conference, the future is bleak and not optimistic. At this time, Japanese naval officers are deliberately preparing, but they are also paying considerable attention to diplomacy, and are no longer willing to fall into the past predicament of being isolated from the world. According to the naval authorities' analysis of the claims of the four main countries in the world regarding the Washington and London treaties, as follows:

(1) It believes that Britain has no intention of changing the London Naval Treaty and the Washington Naval Treaty in terms of quantity, and even intends to continue the treaty in principle. However, there are two opinions in terms of quality: one is to change the current 35,000-ton battleships to 25,000 tons, and the gun caliber is also reduced accordingly; the other is to increase Britain's existing heavy cruisers and light cruisers, from 50 ships to 70 ships.

(2) The United States is the initiator of the Washington Treaty, and its main opinion is to maintain the two treaties. It is very different from Britain's claim. Reducing the tonnage of battleships is beneficial to Britain, but the opposite is true for the United States. Increasing cruisers is also the same, putting the United States in a passive position. Therefore, it advocates extending the naval treaty, or further reducing the existing forces. (3) France has no preference for the claims of Britain and the United States, and its relationship with Japan is also not trivial. What it wants is only equality with Italy on the surface. Between France and Italy, battleships and aircraft carriers are equal, but the French navy is actually dominant. Therefore, it is unwilling to abolish the naval treaty immediately.

(4) Italy is satisfied as long as it is nominally equal to the French navy, because it has financial difficulties and its colonies are limited. Maritime development is only in the Mediterranean. If the naval treaty is abolished and countries start to compete in building navies, Italy will feel the difficulty of coping. Therefore, it does not support abolishing the naval treaty.

According to the above analysis, none of the major countries support abolishing the naval treaty. Isn't Japan going to be in a dilemma? However, it believes that it is very difficult to reconcile Britain and the United States. It will use the discord between Britain and the United States to try its best to sabotage it, and must prevent them from putting forward a new joint proposal. At the same time, it will pay closer attention to the attitudes of Britain and the United States. Now Japan's strategy is that no matter what the opinions of the above four countries are, and regardless of whether the preparatory meeting can succeed, it will propose the abolition of the Washington and London treaties.

Its active claims are: first, it believes that Article 23 of the Washington Treaty, regarding the principle of ratioism, must be abolished. As for the most appropriate time to propose abolition, it is before December 31 of this year; second, it is necessary to establish national defense security, quickly get rid of the shackles of existing unfavorable treaties, and conclude new arms reduction treaties based on the absolute equality of the right to national survival. It is necessary to completely abolish the maintenance of a high degree of armaments and the superiority of armaments in a certain country. Therefore, in the future, the differential ratio should be abolished immediately, and the right of each country to national defense autonomy should be respected, and the reduction of naval armaments should be based on total tonnage. This is the high-sounding statement currently advocated by the Japanese government. Judging from the general situation in Japan, it will never be allowed to cause naval shipbuilding competition with Britain and the United States again. In fact, it is using this kind of high-sounding statement to resist involvement in the political problem, solidify its hegemony in the Far East, and implicitly divide Britain and the United States. We see that the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs has been openly training its diplomats in major European and American countries, instructing them to state to the countries where they are stationed: (1) Japan is sincerely maintaining world peace and wants to reduce the burden on its people and implement arms reduction; (2) Japan intends to reduce offensive weapons such as aircraft carriers and battleships; (3) Japan believes that the principle of ratioism in the Washington Treaty is not suitable for the times, so it advocates equality of armaments among Britain, the United States, and Japan, and advocates that all countries should use total tonnage as the basis for further arms reduction. Such use of diplomatic means is intended to gain the sympathy of Britain, France, and Italy, or at least the goodwill of France and Italy. However, it is very clear that this task is not easy to accomplish and must be dealt with by all parties. Therefore, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs has initiated the organization of an Arms Reduction Information Committee to assist in the progress of arms reduction. The committee is jointly organized by Amau, the director of the Information Department of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, and two section chiefs, Noda, the chairman of the Navy Popularization Committee, and two colonels, and Kudo and Shin, the leaders of the Army Research Committee. It meets once a week to specialize in information work and closely liaises with Japanese military attachés and diplomats stationed in various countries, instructing them on the current needs and points to be noted. These messages are combined to plan a strategy for arms reduction. (September 14, 1934, Tokyo)

Recent Bandit Suppression Situation in Southern Fujian 92

Xiao Jing's Report to the Press

Blockade of Bandit Areas Actively Underway

Xiamen Correspondence: After taking office in Quanzhou, Xiao Jing, the commander of bandit suppression in Southern Fujian, immediately convened a bandit suppression meeting of county magistrates from Quanzhou, Zhangzhou, Xingning, and Yongchun, and focused his efforts on clearing the bandits and communists in Anningyong (i.e., Anxi, Yongchun, and Nan'an counties), because these three counties are where the bandits and communists are most complex and numerous. Xiao came to Xiamen from Quanzhou on the 16th and told reporters about the recent situation of bandit suppression in Anningyong: "The bandits and communists in the three counties are mainly in Anxi, and the situation is complex. There are no less than dozens of gangs of bandits in Anxi, among which the gangs of Lu Zhenshan, Guo Zongzhan, and Fang Zhen are more prominent. These three gangs have about two to three thousand people, and the others are mostly scattered bandits, which will be easy to eliminate. The bandits' nests are in the west of Anxi, the east of Hua'an and Zhangping, and the interior is also extremely complex. There are often internal firefights, because if there is an uneven distribution of the spoils from kidnapping and robbery, they will meet each other with artillery fire," etc. Subsequently, representatives of refugees from Anxi fellow villagers in Xiamen and various townships in Anxi, such as Zhuo Yuanhu and Qiu, went to Xiao's residence (Tianxian Hostel) to petition for troops to suppress the bandits. Xiao came out to comfort them and they dispersed. That evening, the Xiamen Chamber of Commerce hosted a banquet for Xiao, during which Lin Qicheng, the representative of Anxi, reported on the bandit situation in Anxi, saying that in the past two weeks, more than 300 people had been kidnapped and extorted for ransom, and they were all stripped naked to prevent them from escaping, which was an unprecedented example of kidnapping in Southern Fujian. Other instances of burning, killing, and looting are too numerous to mention. The people of Anxi are really in dire straits, and the number of refugees fleeing to Xiamen is increasing day by day, etc. The Bandit Suppression Department has dispatched Ma Hongxing, the commander of the 3rd Security Regiment, to handle the affairs of the bandits and communists in Anningyong, and he set off on the 16th to Yongchun to suppress them. All the security regiments in the three counties are under Ma's command. In addition to suppressing the bandits and communists in Quanzhou and Yongchun, the Bandit Suppression Department is also strictly enforcing a blockade. Quanzhou's smuggled salt is also flooding Anxi and being smuggled into bandit areas, no less than 6,000 catties per day. Xiao Jing recently found out and telegraphed the provincial government on the 15th, saying, "According to the report of Dong Yihuang, the inspector stationed in Anxi to blockade the bandit area, smuggled salt is flooding Anxi, coming from Tong'an via Longmen, and from Anhai via Xiwei, averaging more than 6,000 catties per day, entering Datian Dehua, and transferred to bandit areas. On the same day, the county police in Anxi's Cannai arrested dozens of salt smugglers, who dared to open fire to resist arrest. Xie Shuikuo and Xie Hanlin were arrested, and 25 dans of smuggled salt, weighing 1,795 catties, were seized. The salt criminals have been handed over to the county government for detention," etc. In addition to ordering them to be escorted to the department for strict handling, I report, Xiao Jing.) (17th)

New County Governance Established in Yunnan Province 93

Weixin Changes County Name to Weixin County

Jinhe and Pinghe Merged into Jinping County

Areas Under Lancang Changed to Establishment Zone

Kunming Correspondence: Yunnan Province has a vast area and inconvenient transportation. In addition to the existing 109 counties, 1 city, and 15 establishment bureaus, there are still many remote border areas that are related to national defense or border several counties, and governance is inconvenient. In order to reorganize administrative regions and promote administrative efficiency, the provincial government has decided to transfer the three jia of Shangshu, except for the five- and one-fortress, under the jurisdiction of Zhenxiong, and delineate Shazipo behind Banjugou Liangzibei as the boundary; the middle east, except for the second, fourth, and fifth jia, and then delineate the lower half jia of Shui Tianzhai, the third jia of Zhongdong, with the river as the boundary, to be transferred to Weixin for management and transfer, that is, to establish Weixin as the county seat, and still use the name Weixin, classified as a third-class county, and the original administrative committee will be abolished. The provincial government has issued a clear order to announce it, and selected and appointed a county magistrate to go to receive and establish it. It is hoped that the regional disputes that have been disputed for many years in the two counties can be completely resolved. In addition, the two establishment bureaus of Jinhe and Pinghe are adjacent to Vietnam, and national defense and diplomacy are of great importance. It has been decided to merge the two regions, change the establishment to a county governance, and improve the regime to control it and consolidate the border. It has been found that the total population of the two regions is more than 9,000 households, and the area is also very wide, which is more than enough to set up a county. This time, the merger and change of the county, named Jinping, Mengding has now been changed to Pinghe, so it is named Jinping, temporarily designated as a third-class county. As for the candidate for county magistrate, because it is the first change of county governance, those who are not highly qualified and knowledgeable cannot be competent. The Civil Affairs Department has approved the provincial government to select and appoint Ge Yanchun, the former section chief of the Fourth Section of the Department and the current Political Inspector of the First District, to serve as the county magistrate, and the provincial government committee has approved the appointment after discussion. Ge can go to receive and establish the county governance within days after accepting the appointment. In addition, the four places of Mengjiao, Mengdong, Daoxiang, Haiyan, and Shuai under the jurisdiction of Canglan County are adjacent to Myanmar, with a vast area and many indigenous people under the jurisdiction of the chieftain's office. Because of inconvenient transportation, backward culture, and difficult governance, there are also important relationships with border defense. It is not enough to control it and consolidate the border without setting up a governance as soon as possible. Now, the above four places have been changed to an establishment zone, named Cangyuan, which has also been approved by the provincial government, and Gong Sheng has been appointed as the special commissioner in charge of preparing for the establishment of Cangyuan. He will go to prepare for the establishment on a given date. According to statistics, the wooden seals and seals of the two counties and one establishment zone recently established have been sent by the Civil Affairs Department to the provincial government for initial publication to ensure good faith. After the establishment is established, the facts will be listed separately and submitted to the Ministry of Interior Affairs as a special case, and forwarded to the Executive Yuan for verification and record, and copper seals will be issued to Yunnan to facilitate forwarding and use. (3rd)

Xiamen's Rice Exports Gradually Decreasing 94

Recent Exports Approximately 20,000 Bags

A Decrease Seen Compared to the Previous Month

Xiamen Correspondence: Since the drought in Jiangsu and Zhejiang and the soaring rice prices in Shanghai, Xiamen rice merchants have been competing to transport the stored rice from Zhangzhou to Shanghai for sale. As a result, the rice prices in Xiamen and Zhangzhou once soared by more than two yuan per dan. The Xiamen General Chamber of Commerce once decided to ban rice exports, but the customs authorities could not implement it because they had not received an order from the Ministry, and they continued to ship out rice in succession, but the numbers have been greatly reduced. The statistics of the export of Zhangzhou rice since August 3 are listed below: 130 bags on the Jinan Wheel on August 3, 1,630 bags on the Yuezhou Wheel on the 6th, 1,669 bags on the Fuping Wheel on the 8th, 4,469 bags on the Nanchang Wheel on the 9th, 1,584 bags on the Jinan Wheel on the 17th, 4,919 bags on the Hanjiang Wheel on the 19th, 2,427 bags on the Qingyuan Wheel on the 17th, 7,419 bags on the Yuji Wheel on the 20th, 4,296 bags on the Qiongzhou Wheel on the 20th, 1,984 bags on the Yuda Wheel on the 22nd, 6,257 bags on the Niuzhuang Wheel on the 24th, 3,035 bags on the Guangdong Wheel on the 28th, 7,051 bags on the Tongshang Wheel on the 28th, 4,421 bags on the Jinan Wheel on the 30th, another 5,675 bags on the Yisun Wheel, another 1,985 bags on the Jiahe Wheel, 3,200 bags on the Yuezhou Wheel on September 3, 8,119 bags on the Zhejiang Wheel on the 4th, 2,060 bags on the Luzhou Wheel on the 7th, 4,469 bags on the Nanchang Wheel on the 9th, 1,288 bags on the Hubei Wheel on the 10th, 548 bags on the Tonghua Wheel on the 12th, 150 bags on the Jinan Wheel on the 14th. A total of 58,931 bags were shipped out in August, and a total of 19,834 bags were shipped out in the first half of September, totaling 78,765 bags. Comparing the first half of September with August, the number of shipments has decreased significantly. (17th)

Announcement of the Savings and Custody Committee's Organizational Regulations by the Ministry of Finance 95

Bonds and assets submitted for deposit must be reviewed by the committee.

The committee may advise the Ministry of Finance on deposit custody matters.

Beijing News: The Savings Deposit Guarantee Reserve Custody Committee has been formally established. The organizational regulations of the committee, after being submitted by the Ministry of Finance to the Executive Yuan for review, were approved by the Executive Yuan meeting the day before yesterday. Yesterday, the Ministry of Finance announced them by ministerial order. The entire document consists of thirteen articles. The original text is recorded below: (Article 1) The Ministry of Finance establishes the Savings Deposit Guarantee Reserve Custody Committee to implement the provisions of Article 9 of the Savings Bank Law and to enhance the bank's reputation. The committee is responsible for supervising and inspecting the custody of savings deposit guarantee reserves. (Article 2) When a savings bank submits bonds or other assets, the type, quantity, and value must be reviewed and approved by the committee before being deposited into the treasury. The same applies to exchanges. (Article 3) The committee will conduct a vault inspection once at the end of each month and may conduct inspections at any time when necessary. (Article 4) The committee will consist of seven members: one appointed by the Ministry of Finance, two appointed by the Central Bank, two recommended by member banks of the Shanghai Banking Association, and two designated by the Ministry of Finance from non-member banks and savings associations. The Ministry of Finance will also designate one of the members as chairman. (Article 5) The committee will have one secretary and several staff members, concurrently filled by employees of the Central Bank. (Article 6) The committee will hold a regular meeting every half month. When necessary, the chairman may decide to convene a temporary meeting, or it may be convened at the request of two or more members. (Article 7) When a member cannot attend a committee meeting due to business, they may authorize a representative to attend in writing. If the chairman is absent due to business, the members may mutually elect one person as temporary chairman. (Article 8) A quorum of more than half of the committee members is required to convene a meeting, and a majority vote of the attending members is required to resolve matters. In the event of a tie, the chairman will decide. (Article 9) The committee may make recommendations to the Ministry of Finance regarding the custody of savings deposit guarantee reserves. (Article 10) At the end of each month, the committee shall submit a list to the Ministry of Finance for record-keeping, detailing the types, quantities, and values of bonds and other assets submitted by the savings bank during that month. (Article 11) The minutes of the committee meetings shall be signed by the chairman and kept by the committee. (Article 12) The committee may formulate its own rules of procedure, but they must be submitted to the Ministry of Finance for approval. (Article 13) These regulations shall be implemented by the Ministry of Finance with the approval of the Executive Yuan. The same applies when revisions are made.

Public and Legal Organizations in Wuxi Again Request Suspension of Urban Land Price Declaration 96

The Jiangsu Provincial Government recently held urban land price declarations in Wuxi and Nantong counties. After hearing the news, all sectors of Wuxi opposed it. The request was not approved. The other day, public and legal organizations again sent telegrams to Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, President Wang Jingwei, Provincial Chairman Chen, and Directors Yu and Zhao, requesting an immediate order to suspend the urban land price declaration. The original telegram is as follows: (Zhenjiang, Jiangsu Provincial Government Chairman Chen, Civil Affairs Director Yu, Finance Director Zhao Junjian: We received your government's order No. 19 of the Land Department, regarding our previous telegram requesting the suspension of land price declaration due to local hardship. The order stated: "Your telegram has been noted. Land price declaration is of utmost importance to national economy and people's livelihood. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek convened senior administrative personnel from all provinces in Nanchang in March of this year and repeatedly instructed them to plan for the immediate collection of urban land tax, emphasizing its great significance and the urgency of the work. The government, upholding Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's intention to create welfare for the people and closely observing the actual local situation, is conducting urban land price declarations to develop people's livelihood and promote social prosperity. This does not violate the grand principles of national reconstruction and can be expected to realize Dr. Sun Yat-sen's teachings at an early date. We hope you will understand this intention and provide your support. This order is hereby given." After receiving this order, we learned that Jiangsu Province is conducting urban land price declarations with the intention of creating welfare for the people as instructed by Chairman Chiang Kai-shek. If it can indeed develop people's livelihood and promote social prosperity, we would naturally comply and would not dare to trouble you again. However, we recently saw a news report from Zhenjiang on the 4th of this month, which stated that Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's Nanchang Headquarters issued Directive No. 1244 of the Review Department. The second item in your government's instructions to Jiangsu Province stated: "Land survey is the starting point for land consolidation and an important task for completing self-government. It should be expedited within the possible scope to complete the task as soon as possible. The existing results of land investigation in Zhenjiang and other counties should be promoted to other counties to assist in tax consolidation." Furthermore, public and legal organizations in our county and both the Beijing and Shanghai native-place associations have successively received approvals from Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's Nanchang Headquarters, instructing them to directly submit their requests to the competent authorities in the province for review and handling. After carefully interpreting Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's directive, it seems that it is indeed based on Dr. Sun Yat-sen's teachings, recognizing land survey as the starting point for land consolidation and confirming it as an important task for completing self-government. Even if urban land tax should be planned for collection, it is appropriate to start with land consolidation first. Since land survey is underway in Jiangsu Province, it is appropriate to strictly follow Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's directive, endeavoring to expedite land survey within the possible scope to complete self-government and realize Dr. Sun Yat-sen's teachings. The reason why the Fundamentals of National Reconstruction stipulates land price declaration and the collection of land price tax as tasks for the beginning of self-government is that, at the beginning of self-government, the people, in accordance with the Fundamentals of National Reconstruction, must fulfill their obligations of paying land price tax and land value increment for the local area, and also have the right to directly elect and recall officials and create and reject laws. The rights and obligations are actually reciprocal. The true spirit of the Three Principles of the People lies in this, and the important significance of revolutionary work also lies in this. Moreover, what is collected from the local area is still used for the local area. Therefore, it is said that the entire county shares and the local area owns. Since self-government is based on the county as a unit, the determination of land price must be for the entire county before the local area can enjoy it, and then the entire county can realize Dr. Sun Yat-sen's teachings. Realization depends on promoting self-government and is definitely not a matter for a partial corner of the city to declare and handle in advance. As for Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's directive that land investigation should be promoted in Zhenjiang and other counties, it is not clear whether it is the same as the land price declaration currently being conducted in Wuxi and other places. We cannot speculate. However, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's directive is to assist in tax consolidation. Referring to the land investigation in Yixing and other counties as reported in the newspaper, any excess land is used to reduce the tax burden of the entire county. This is specifically for tax consolidation and to equalize the local burden. It should not be confused with the land price declaration currently being conducted in Wuxi and other places, which is for the collection of land price tax and land value increment tax. What the people are alarmed about is not the land price declaration itself, but the collection of land price tax and land value increment tax after the land price declaration. Recently, urban residents have been spreading rumors, saying that supervisors are bringing police to the door. If the head of the household is away on business, the declaration form is not handed over to the residents, and they are left to declare it themselves. Only women and children are briefly questioned, and the form is filled out on their behalf, ordering them to imprint or stamp it before leaving. If this is the case, can it be used as a basis for future taxation, and will the residents also recognize it as valid? This seems to be worth studying. Moreover, only if the local area can truly prosper can land value increase. The silk industry in Wuxi has failed, and agriculture and commerce have been in difficulty in recent years. Coupled with continuous years of disasters, land prices have undoubtedly fallen. How can simply declaring land prices develop people's livelihood? You, as leaders seeking to govern for the people, should be able to understand the people's suffering. We propose that you strictly follow Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's directive. If it is for land consolidation, you should immediately start land survey. If it is for tax consolidation, you should also conduct land investigation. Choose one of the two to conduct on a trial basis first. As for determining land prices and collecting land taxes, you should still follow Dr. Sun Yat-sen's teachings and listen to local self-government. This will not violate the grand principles of national reconstruction and can be expected to realize Dr. Sun Yat-sen's teachings. This matter concerns the well-being of the people, and it is difficult to remain silent. We believe that in a prosperous nation, the people's suffering should not be concealed. We hereby express our firm opinions again, hoping that you will adopt them and temporarily suspend the declaration to relieve the people's livelihood and honor the legacy. We are extremely apprehensive. Qian Jihou, Director of the Public Funds and Property Management Office of Wuxi County; Chen Zuolin, Deputy Director; Yang Choumei, Chairman of the Chamber of Commerce; Cai Wenxin, Qian Jihou, Chen Zuolin, Wu Shimei, Current Affairs Committee Members; Qian Zhongliang, Chief of the First District; Tao Guanshi, Du Puchen, Gu Hongzhi, Deng Yufen, Wang Jinghui, Tang Jiyun, Yang Hanxi, Wu Xiangqing, Hua Chun'an, Chen Zikuan, Zhou Guanxiong, Shao Qinbang, Shi Binzhang, Jiang Zumin, Xu Songru, Hua Ti, Liu Hongkun, Cheng Yuming, Yu Xiangxian, Wen Qiyin, Chen Shaoqin, Miao Dongchen, Cai Huchen, Zhao Zixin, Cai Jihui, Chen Hanxiang, Xie Yongnan, Shen Chucai, Feng Yaoxing, Cheng Jingtang, Yao Ganshi, Xu Jingyuan, Qin Yuanzhao, Zhu Jianshan, Zhou Qichang, and 267 Deputy Township Chiefs and Supervisory Committee Members, jointly kowtow. A separate submission to Chairman Chiang Kai-shek of the Nanchang Headquarters and President Wang Jingwei of the Executive Yuan is also roughly the same. Omitted for brevity.

The county's Anti-Smoking Committee stated that the deadline for registering smokers is the 15th of this month. The district's opium dens have generally decided on how to establish sales and smoking locations, but the allocation decision must wait until after the registration deadline. The application deadline for sales and smoking locations is the 25th. Three opium warehouses should be established in the county, one each in the city, Fengjing, and Tinglin. Autumn Rice Discovers Leafhoppers and Mold Spots 99

This year, the weather has been extremely dry, and most rice seedlings have withered. Less than 50% of the fields in the four townships have been able to pump water for transplanting. Recently, due to heavy autumn rains, leafhoppers have become even more severe in the rice paddies, and mold spots have appeared on the rice husks, which are hollow and without substance. The autumn harvest in low-lying fields is feared to be hopeless. Yesterday, Qian Sunqing, director of the County Funds and Property Office, specially attached a clump of autumn rice and requested that special attention be paid during the upcoming autumn inspection, not to assume that there is a harvest simply because all the fields appear to have rice. Two Ships Robbed En Route 102

Ships between Changzhou and Heqiao (Yixing jurisdiction) loaded passengers and cargo from Heqiao at 5:00 PM on the 18th and set sail for Changzhou as usual. Around 3:00 AM in the middle of the night when they were near the Fifteen-Hole Bridge, six robbers suddenly appeared on the shore. At this time, a ship from Tingqiao Bridge arrived, and the robbers split up and boarded the ship to search for valuables. All the cash hidden by the boat owners and passengers was robbed. Fortunately, no one was injured. After the robbery, the robbers went ashore and howled northward. Passenger Crushed to Death on Baohua Steamer 107

Zhang Caifu from Qidong Antougang was a cook at Yao Shaofu's shipyard in Shanghai. On the 12th of this month, he returned to Qidong on the Baohua Steamer of the Ping An Company. Unemployed Student Commits Suicide 108

Chang Guanglin from Sichuan, currently residing in Beiping, is 26 years old and graduated from the University of Paris in France. After returning to China in 1932, he worked as a staff member of the Kunming Municipal Government in Yunnan. He later resigned for some reason and was unemployed at home. This summer, he came to Shanghai to seek employment but was unsuccessful. He pawned all his luggage and clothes. The day before yesterday, he boarded the Baofeng Steamer to Haimen. When the ship reached the vicinity of Sanhegang, he suddenly jumped into the river, intending to commit suicide. Fortunately, a waiter saw him and immediately stopped the ship to rescue him, and he was saved. The passengers then donated 25 silver dollars as travel expenses for him to return to Beiping. Chang then boarded the original ship back to Shanghai.

Military Department Cracks Down on Military Forcibly Requisitioning Trains 117

Circular Posted at Various Stations by the Two Railways Bureau

Previously, the Two Railways Bureau found it difficult when various troops, using the railway for transportation, often did not follow prescribed procedures, failing to consult the Ministry of Military Affairs and the Ministry of Railways before requisitioning trains, and instead forcibly demanding loading and transportation. The Bureau reported the actual situation to the Ministry of Railways, requesting that it consult the Ministry of Military Affairs to issue a proclamation to be posted at various stations to prevent this. The original text of the Ministry of Military Affairs' proclamation reads: "Upon investigation, if military organizations or troops have transfer matters requiring the use of vehicles, they should follow the prescribed procedures and methods stipulated in the Railway Military Transport Regulations. They must not directly demand vehicle transportation from railway stations. For transportation via the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo railways, those departing from Beijing Station or Hangzhou Station, as well as stations along the Beijing-Hangzhou route, must first report to this Ministry, which will then request the Ministry of Railways to order the railway to prepare transportation. Those who do not comply with these procedures and directly demand trains from railway stations will be refused loading and transportation. Any acts of forcible requisitioning of trains will be investigated and punished according to law to uphold regulations. In addition to issuing separate orders, this proclamation is hereby issued for general knowledge, and all are expected to strictly comply without violation. This proclamation."

Jiangsu Provincial Government Borrows Money from Shanghai Banks 118

For Grain Storage to Prevent Famine

Agreed Upon with Five Banks

According to New Voice News Agency, the Jiangsu Provincial Government, recognizing that this year's autumn harvest in Taixing, Taizhou, Gaoyou, Yancheng, Xinghua, and other areas in northern Jiangsu is very abundant, while southern Jiangsu is suffering from drought and famine, has instructed Zhao Dihua, Director of the Department of Finance, to contact five banks in Shanghai – the Bank of China, Bank of Communications, Shanghai Commercial & Savings Bank, Jiangsu Bank, and Farmers Bank of China – to borrow money for grain storage to prevent famine. The plan is to first purchase grain from rice-producing areas in northern Jiangsu.

Kong Xiangxi Returns to Shanghai and Discusses My Thorough Investigation of the Arms Case in the United States 119

Absolutely No Truth to the Rumor of Using American Loans to Exchange for Arms

No Need to Be Discouraged by Failing to Be Elected to the League of Nations

According to the Central News Agency, Kong Xiangxi, Vice President of the Executive Yuan, arrived in Shanghai last morning at 7:30 a.m. via an overnight train from Beijing the previous evening at 11:00 p.m. He went directly to his private residence on Seymour Road to rest. Later, at around 10:00 a.m., he went to the Central Bank to work. In the afternoon at 4:00 p.m., he attended the board meeting of the Central Bank. Wu Tiecheng, the mayor of Shanghai, visited Kong Xiangxi yesterday evening and discussed matters for about 20 minutes before leaving. Kong Xiangxi then met with reporters and made the following remarks:

Thoroughly Investigate the Arms Commission Issue 120

According to Kong Xiangxi, regarding the announcement by the U.S. Senate's Munitions Investigation Committee concerning a letter from the DuPont arms company's representative in China, which claimed that when arms were sold to China, some Chinese officials and generals received commissions, Chiang Kai-shek and President Wang Jingwei have paid close attention to this matter. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs has instructed Shi Zhaoji, the ambassador to the United States, to inform the U.S. Department of State and request that Senator Nye, chairman of the U.S. Senate's Munitions Investigation Committee, immediately publish the names of the Chinese officials and generals mentioned in the letter from the DuPont company's representative in China who allegedly received commissions. If this is indeed the case, a thorough investigation will be conducted. As for Chairman Nye's claim that China used $20 million in American cotton and wheat loans to exchange for arms from Italy, this is completely untrue. The cotton, wheat, and flour that China borrowed from the United States were successively shipped to Shanghai and sold, and the resulting cash was entirely used by the National Economic Council for construction purposes. The facts are there and can be proven. To say that China purchased arms from Italy and then immediately claim that this was a misappropriation of American cotton and wheat loans is absurd. If you see me buying a penny's worth of peanuts, can you immediately say that this penny was stolen from the Central Bank? It is regrettable that such untrue statements came from the mouth of the chairman of the U.S. Senate's Munitions Investigation Committee.

We Should Know to Strengthen Ourselves from Failing to be Elected to the League of Nations 121

As for our country's failure to be re-elected as a non-permanent member of the League of Nations, I am deeply saddened. However, the people of our country should not be discouraged by this. We must work hard to strengthen ourselves, and then one day, even if our country does not compete, it will surely be elected. Do you not see the Soviet Union today? The Soviet Union is a socialist country that was once incompatible with the capitalist countries of Europe. Now, after years of struggle, the Soviet Union has reached a state of prosperity and strength, so European countries invited it to join the League of Nations and elected it as a permanent member. If the people of our country can strive to strengthen themselves, our international standing will naturally increase. Why would it be limited to just being elected as a non-permanent member of the League of Nations?

Old Revenue Stamps Will Never Be Exchanged 122

In the past, merchants would sometimes buy revenue stamps, fulfilling their tax obligations, but then store the stamps in boxes without affixing them. There were even cases of buying stamps today and reselling them to others tomorrow, or taking old stamps to places where stamps were affixed for sale. The Ministry of Finance, in order to prevent these abuses, in addition to printing regional designations on the stamps, has decided to abolish accumulated old stamps and declare them invalid starting from November 1st, and issue new tax stamps. This decision was made at the National Financial Conference convened in June. At that time, after the abolition of miscellaneous taxes, the local governments' finances were expected to experience panic, so the central government decided to allocate one-third of the original central revenue stamp tax revenue to subsidize local governments, one-tenth to subsidize provincial governments, and two-tenths to subsidize border provincial governments. The old stamps would be abolished, declared invalid, and new revenue stamps would be issued and strictly affixed. However, in order to alleviate the difficulties of merchants, the central government originally planned to implement this on September 1st, but because the new stamps have not yet been printed, the implementation has been postponed to November. Requests from local chambers of commerce to exchange accumulated old stamps for new stamps, extending the validity of old stamps until the end of this year, are unreasonable and will not be approved by the Ministry of Finance. In the future, the issuance of new stamps will be handled by post offices, and local governments will supervise merchants' affixation.

Prize Savings Will Be Immediately Banned 123

Regarding the prohibition of prize savings, the Ministry of Finance is currently studying sound measures and will implement them as soon as a decision is made.

Agreement Reached on Overall Cooperation 124

Director Zhao has now contacted the five banks to discuss the amount of the loan. The provincial government plans to borrow one million yuan, but the banks are willing to lend 200,000 to 300,000 yuan first, depending on the amount of grain purchased. The purchased grain will serve as collateral. However, it is stipulated that the provincial government will allocate funds to cover losses. The contract will be signed after negotiations are completed.

Commencement of Purchases 125

After the banks agreed to the grain storage loan, the provincial government, recognizing that new rice has already entered the market in rice-producing areas in northern Jiangsu, will allocate 50,000 yuan and send staff to purchase it. In the future, it will be sold at a fixed price to facilitate regulation. This loan for grain storage is of a pilot nature. If it proves successful in the future, the scope will be expanded.
